﻿Very Simple Sales Letter Outline:
* Hook/Microlead
* Lead
* Background (Credibility and Origin Story)
* Discovery
* UMP/UMS
* Product Build-Up and Reveal
* Close
* FAQ

Example Formats: 
6 Minute VSL
Will return to this.

15 Minute VSL
Eg 1: https://docs.google.com/document/d/1BAESwq17ji50IuO7Wq0-snyp-yZHI4rKZwSSTBD8dEA/edit?usp=sharing

Eg2: 
https://docs.google.com/document/d/1eYZkzKYmez-SAmAmlipHv69n2xkeWIdZcqISfoEug4c/edit?usp=sharing

35 Minute VSL:
https://youtu.be/ewH5uZVjaAY?si=39SX6xu_set5RG56

Sales Letter Outline: 

* Support points - you don't necessarily have to use everything
** The order within a point is not necessarily in that order - they can also “mix” with each other

1. Pre-Lead/MicroLead
1. -Hook heavy or attention grabbing opening line. 
2. - Quickly related to the pain-point prospect faces 
3. - Quick related to the promise of a solution 

Nooro Ads Library:
https://www.facebook.com/ads/library/?active_status=all&ad_type=all&country=US&view_all_page_id=107580105023479&search_type=page&media_type=all

Nooro Similar Web:
https://pro.similarweb.com/?#/digitalsuite/websiteanalysis/referrals/incoming-traffic/*/999/3m?webSource=Total&key=nooro-us.com

2. Lead (These Don’t Have to be in order) (Open a bunch of loops with fascinations, and say - I’m going to get to that in just a moment, or a few minutes, or “and you’ll see that in this video”
   1. Call Out Problem 
   2. Promise Solution to Pain Point + Promise to Save Time/Money 
   3. Tease Emotional Discovery Story 
   4. Tease Unique Mechanism Behind Solution 
   5. Tease Contrarian Nature of Mechanism (This Flies in the Face of What You’ve Been Told Before)
   6. Working in “Fascinations” as Incentive For Continuing With Copy (I’ll Answer This Riddle For You)
   7. Briefly Mention Credibility Builders
   8. Qualifiers – Who This Works For. Is It For Everyone? Is It For a Certain Subset? Speak to Your Market. 
   9. Briefly Address Skepticism.  
   10. Include a Few Broad Testimonials if Available (About Benefits But Don’t Give Away Product)

3. II. Background Story
   1. Who I Am + Credibility Builders When Appropriate (ie. A Doctor or Expert) 
   2. “Me or Someone Close to Me Was Just Like You (In Pain)” – Here’s The Emotional Story About It
   3. Traditional Solutions & Advice Not Working
   4. Trigger Event – Problem or Pain Point Escalated to Where Avatar Realizes Something MUST Change
   5. Search for Truth/Answers 

   4. III. Unique Mechanism of the Problem

      1. Explaining the “Real Cause” of the Problem; You’ve Had 99% of the Answer But This is the Missing 1%  
      2. Should Be Surprising, Possibly Even Counterintuitive 
      3. Backed by Credibility and Proof Elements 

         5. Unique Mechanism of The Solution
         1. Now That You Know the Real Cause of the Problem, This is the “Real Solution” on a MACRO level. 
         2. This Should Be Logically Connected to the Problem 
         3. Once They Have the MACRO Solution (A Theory) – They Dig Deep To Prove The Theory (And Get Into The MICRO). 
         4. Backed By Credibility and Proof Elements, Including Citations and Scientific Sources.

            6.  V. Product Buildup + Reveal

               1. Now That Avatar Knows The Solution, He Looks For An “Out-of-the-Box” Version; Something That Will Just End His Quest and Solve The Problem Right There
               2. But Discovers That Out-of-the-Box Is Flawed 
               3. Has to Do It Himself And Create Novel New Solution
               4. Starts Testing It or Working On It. There Are Problems and Setbacks
               5. But Eventual Success/Breakthrough
               6. Proof Product Works
               7. Others Asking For It
               8. PRODUCT Is Born!

               7. VI. Close 

                  1. Product Details (What’s Included, What Makes it Special, Unique Selling Propositions)
                  2. Discuss and Dismiss Other Alternatives (Expensive, Ineffective, Side-Effects, Poor Quality, Unproven)
                  3. Keep Building Up Value of -PRODUCT-
                  4. Additional Testimonials
                  5. How to Use The Product
                  6. Scarcity: Demand Is High, Supplies Are Limited, Out-of-Stocks Are Common
                  7. Personal Mission of Avatar to Make Things Better – Tied to Emotion
                  8. Price Justification & Reveal – Other “Solutions” Are More Expensive & Consequences of Inaction are Costly (Cost Can Be Either Material or Immaterial)
                  9. This Solution is Better and Will Save You Money, It’s Normally $X Which is Bargain, But Right Now You Can Get It For Just $Y!
                  10. Smart People Buy More

                  8. First Call to Action 
                  1. What Happens After You Click The Button
                  2. Optional: Valuable Free Bonuses Revealed
                  3. Guarantee – You’ll Most Likely Have a Great Experience, But If For Any Reason You Don’t, No Risk and No Hassle

                  9. Second Call to Action 
                  1. Two Choices – You Can Go On Suffering, Or You Can Take Action Today and Change Your Life forever; The Choice Is Yours
                  2. Urgency 2 – But You Really Must Hurry As This is The End of the Presentation And There’s No Guarantee How Long Offer Will Be Available

                  10. Third Call to Action 
                  1. Thank You For Watching

                  11. VII. FAQs
                  1. Back to Being Their Friend; Helping To Clear Up Any Confusion They May Have
                  2. Reminding Them of What Product Is, What It’s Used For, Importance of Taking Action Today, Terms of Guarantee, and How to Buy!

================================================================================
FILE: 29_Long_Form_VSL_Create_Lesson_DOC_66.txt
================================================================================

﻿Unity Eye Serum VSL Brief - Opal Beauty
1. Who's the Audience?
Primary Target: Problem-aware and solution-aware women aged 35-60+ (peak target: 40-55)
Demographics:
* Generation X and younger Baby Boomers
* Middle to upper-middle class with disposable income for premium skincare ($50k+ household income)
* Peak earning years, often "Sandwich Generation" caring for children and aging parents
* Self-appointed "Chief Medical Officer" of household with sophisticated health/beauty literacy
* Heavy online researchers who read reviews extensively before purchasing
* Active on Facebook, increasingly on TikTok/Instagram for beauty content
Psychographics:
* Shocked by sudden appearance of aging signs: "I wake up one day and notice something new—a line where there wasn't one before"
* Feel betrayed by their changing body/face and don't recognize themselves
* Frustrated by trial-and-error exhaustion with products that don't work
* Experiencing identity crisis around aging in a youth-obsessed culture
* Sophisticated consumers who distrust marketing hype but respond to science
2. What are the pain points, or biggest fears?
PRIMARY PAIN POINTS (The Big 3):
1. Sudden, Shocking Appearance of Eye Aging Signs

   * Crow's feet, under-eye wrinkles, and puffiness that seemed to appear "overnight"
   * Dark circles making them look perpetually tired
   * Crepey, loose skin that's lost its "snap" and firmness
   2. Loss of Identity and Confidence

      * No longer turning heads or feeling attractive
      * Avoiding photos and mirrors
      * Looking older than they feel inside
      * Fear of becoming invisible or irrelevant in society
      3. Financial Frustration from Failed Solutions

         * Spending hundreds/thousands on eye creams that don't work
         * Feeling scammed by expensive department store products
         * Fear of wasting more money on another disappointing product
Secondary Pain Points:
         * Short Term: Daily makeup taking longer, concealer not working, looking tired at work
         * Long Term: Fear of accelerating aging, loss of professional relevance, relationship insecurities
3. Big promises about how this sales copy will change their lives forever
Teaser Promises for the VSL itself:
         * "I'm going to reveal the hidden reason why your eye creams have failed you—and it's not what you think"
         * "You'll discover the breakthrough science that explains why your eyes age faster than the rest of your face"
         * "I'll show you the one missing piece that makes all the difference between products that work and products that waste your money"
         * "By the end of this presentation, you'll understand exactly what to look for in an eye treatment—and why this changes everything"
4. What Does It Look Like When A Prospect's Pain Points Have Been Solved?
Visual Transformation:
         * Eyes that look bright, rested, and alert—matching how they feel inside
         * Smooth, firm skin that has regained its "bounce" and elasticity
         * Dramatically reduced crow's feet and under-eye wrinkles
         * Lighter, brighter under-eye area free from dark circles and puffiness
         * Confident enough to go makeup-free or with minimal concealer
Emotional Empowerment:
         * Feeling attractive and confident in their own skin again
         * Looking in the mirror and recognizing themselves
         * Receiving compliments about looking refreshed and youthful
         * Professional confidence restored—commanding respect and attention
         * Freedom from the anxiety of aging
Lifestyle Benefits:
         * Faster morning routine—no need for heavy concealer
         * Confidence in photos and social situations
         * Peace of mind knowing they've found a solution that actually works
         * Financial relief from ending the cycle of expensive disappointments
5. What solutions for the reader's problem exist already (and why aren't they working)?
Mass Market Eye Creams (CeraVe, Olay, Neutrogena)
         * What they tried: Basic moisturizers marketed for eye area
         * Why inadequate: Generic formulations, minimal active ingredients, don't address root causes
Prestige Department Store Brands (Estée Lauder, Clinique, La Mer)
         * What they tried: Higher-priced creams with basic anti-aging ingredients
         * Why inadequate: Overpriced for results, heavy textures, outdated formulations, paying for packaging
Professional Treatments (Botox, Fillers, Laser)
         * What they tried: In-office procedures
         * Why inadequate: Expensive ($500-2000+), temporary (3-6 months), unnatural appearance, requires ongoing maintenance
Budget "Active" Serums (The Ordinary, CeraVe)
         * What they tried: Affordable serums with retinol, vitamin C
         * Why inadequate: Often too harsh, cause irritation, basic formulations, trial-and-error frustration
High-End "Miracle" Creams ($200-500)
         * What they tried: Luxury products with premium marketing
         * Why inadequate: "Hope in a jar" with minimal innovation, paying for brand name not efficacy
6. Unique Mechanism of the Problem and Unique Mechanism of the Solution
UNIQUE MECHANISM OF THE PROBLEM: "Collagen Architecture Breakdown"
The real reason eye creams fail isn't just collagen loss—it's Collagen Architecture Breakdown happening at the Dermal-Epidermal Junction (DEJ).
Think of young skin like high-quality fabric with a perfectly tight, organized weave. Every collagen "thread" is in its proper place, working together to create smooth, strong, beautiful skin.
But as we age, something far more devastating occurs than simple thread loss. Those collagen threads don't just disappear—they become loose, tangled, and lose their organized structure. This breakdown begins at the DEJ, where your skin layers meet, and spreads throughout the collagen matrix.
Instead of that tight, precise weave, your skin's foundation becomes like fabric that's been stretched and twisted until the threads are jumbled together. When this organized structure collapses, it creates gaps and weaknesses in the skin's foundation. These structural failures mean:
         * The skin's support network can no longer hold its shape, causing sagging and wrinkles
         * Nutrients can't travel efficiently through the disorganized matrix
         * Dark circles appear as the weakened structure allows blood vessels to show through
         * Fluid accumulates in the gaps where organized structure once provided drainage
         * Skin loses its firm, youthful "snap" because the underlying architecture can no longer bounce back
UNIQUE MECHANISM OF THE SOLUTION: "The Structural Renewal System"
The breakthrough solution isn't to add more collagen to broken fabric—it's to restore the organized structure of the weave itself through our three-step Structural Renewal System:
Step 1: The Structural Renewal Signal Dipalmitoyl Hydroxyproline acts like a master weaver, commanding your skin's machinery to pull loose, tangled collagen threads taut and reorganize them back into their proper weave. Modified with palmitic acid, it penetrates deep to where structural damage exists.
Step 2: The Targeted Repair Complex Precise amino acids (Proline, Glycine, Alanine) provide exact building blocks for collagen synthesis—not random proteins, but the specific materials your skin needs to rebuild the organized structure.
Step 3: The Integrity Locking System The same compounds inhibit matrix metalloproteinases (the enzymes that destroy collagen architecture), protecting your newly restored structure from future breakdown.
7. Unique Nickname for the Unique Mechanism
"The Structural Renewal System"
Teaser phrases:
         * "The 3-step skin unifying system that rebuilds your eye area from the inside out"
         * "The structural renewal breakthrough that reverses collagen architecture breakdown"
         * "The collagen architecture discovery that's changing everything about eye aging"
8. Main Ingredients and Studies
Dipalmitoyl Hydroxyproline:
         * Clinical study: 32% reduction in wrinkles, 14% increase in skin firmness
         * Stimulates TIMP production, reducing collagen-degrading enzymes by 33% (trypsin) and 22% (elastase)
         * At 0.5% concentration shows measurable wrinkle depth improvement
Pistacia Lentiscus Extract (Mastic):
         * Increases density of supporting fibers in upper dermis by 51%
         * Decreases weakened dermal layer by 29%
         * 80% COX-2 inhibition, 20% LOX inhibition for anti-inflammatory effects
Saccharide Isomerate:
         * 55% increase in skin hydration lasting up to 72 hours
         * 20% reduction in transepidermal water loss after 28 days
         * 20% improvement in dry skin signs
Sodium Hyaluronate:
         * 134% immediate increase in skin water content
         * 63% improvement in hydration, 60% plumping effect after 6 weeks
         * Clinical trials show excellent tolerability across all skin types
Cupuacu Seed Butter:
         * 440% water absorption capacity (exceeds lanolin and shea butter)
         * 86% decrease in xerosis, 55% decrease in skin tears in clinical studies
         * Stimulates cell proliferation and migration in dermal fibroblasts
Vitamin C & E:
         * Vitamin C: Essential for collagen synthesis, 10% sodium ascorbate improves eyelid thickness
         * Combined C+E: 4-8 fold increase in UV protection, significant wrinkle reduction
9. Bold Product Claims
Primary Results Claims:
         * Visibly reduce crow's feet and fine lines by up to 39% in just 4 weeks
         * Brighten dark circles and restore even skin tone around eyes
         * Lift and firm sagging under-eye bags for a more youthful appearance
         * Restore skin's natural "snap" and elasticity that you thought was gone forever
         * Achieve professional-grade results without the professional price or procedures
Emotional Transformation Claims:
         * Look as refreshed and vibrant as you feel inside
         * Regain confidence to go makeup-free or with minimal concealer
         * Turn heads again and receive compliments about looking well-rested
         * Feel in control of your aging process instead of victimized by it
         * Skip the concealer and enjoy faster, easier morning routines
10. What is the Product?
Unity Eye Revive Serum by Opal Beauty
Core Features:
         * 0.5 fl oz precision-dispensed bottle designed for delicate eye area application
         * Lightweight, fast-absorbing serum texture that works beautifully under makeup
         * Clean formulation free from parabens, phthalates, synthetic fragrances, silicones
         * Small-batch crafted for quality assurance in USA facilities
Key Benefits & Fascinations:
         * Penetrates deep into the Dermal-Epidermal Junction where eye aging begins
         * Features six clinically-proven ingredients working in synergy
         * The only eye treatment targeting collagen architecture breakdown

﻿Unity Eye Serum VSL Script (27-Minute Long-Form)
Pre-Lead/Microlead Options
Option #1
If you're a woman over 35 who's been shocked by the sudden appearance of crow's feet, under-eye wrinkles, or dark circles that make you look exhausted even when you're well-rested...
And you've tried expensive eye creams, department store "miracles," even professional treatments, but nothing seems to work...
Then what I'm about to reveal will be the most important breakthrough you'll ever discover for transforming your eye area and getting back the youthful, confident look you deserve.
So please, watch this short presentation to the very end. I promise it will be worth your while.

Option #2
Here's why using eye creams with collagen is a mistake...
If you're a woman over 35 who's been spending money on collagen eye creams, expensive department store "miracles," or even professional treatments, but your crow's feet keep getting deeper and those dark circles won't go away...
You're making the same costly mistake that I made for years - pouring new ingredients onto broken structure.
Think about it like this: if you had a beautifully woven sweater that unraveled into a pile of tangled yarn, would throwing more yarn on top fix it? Of course not. You'd need to reorganize the threads back into their proper structure.
That's exactly what's happening to your eye area, and why every collagen cream has failed you.
What I'm about to reveal will be the most important breakthrough you'll ever discover for transforming your eye area - and it has nothing to do with adding more collagen to the mess.
So please, watch this short presentation to the very end, because what you're about to learn will save you thousands of dollars and years of disappointment.

Option #3
Pre-Lead/MicroLead

And you're still dealing with crow's feet that seem to get deeper every month, dark circles that make you look exhausted, and that crepey under-eye skin that makes you avoid close-up photos...
Then you've fallen for the biggest lie in the beauty industry.
The truth is, when your skin's underlying structure has collapsed, price doesn't matter - approach does. That $400 eye cream is targeting the completely wrong problem.
What I'm about to reveal will be the most important breakthrough you'll ever discover for transforming your eye area without breaking the bank or falling for expensive false promises.
So please, watch this short presentation to the very end. I promise it will save you from making another costly mistake.

Option #4
Stop using collagen creams until you watch this...
If you're a woman over 35 who's been religiously applying collagen eye creams, spending hundreds on "proven" formulas, or layering product after product around your delicate eye area...
But your crow's feet keep getting deeper, those dark circles won't budge, and that under-eye skin feels thinner and more fragile every month...
Then you need to understand what's really happening beneath your skin.
The real reason your eyes age faster than the rest of your face isn't about needing MORE collagen. Think of your skin like a perfectly woven fabric - but after 35, the entire structure starts collapsing into a tangled mess.
Pouring more collagen on broken architecture is like throwing new threads onto a pile of yarn and expecting it to become a sweater. It simply doesn't work.

So please, watch this short presentation to the very end, because this changes everything you thought you knew about anti-aging.

Lead - Opening Multiple Loops
Hi, my name is Laura. And I want to talk about that devastating moment. The one that happens to so many of us. It’s when you look in the mirror one morning… and you just don't recognize the tired, aged face staring back at you.
Maybe for you, it was the crow's feet that seemed to appear overnight. Or the dark circles that no amount of sleep or concealer can seem to hide. Or maybe it’s that delicate skin under your eyes that’s become thin and crepey… losing its 'snap.' It's a feeling of betrayal. You feel vibrant and youthful on the inside, but your eyes are telling a different story.
But here's what I want you to imagine for just a moment...
Picture waking up tomorrow morning and looking in the mirror to see bright, rested eyes that actually match how vibrant you feel inside.
Imagine being confident enough to go completely makeup-free, or using just a tiny dab of concealer instead of layers and layers trying to hide the damage.
Picture receiving genuine compliments from friends saying "You look so refreshed! Did you get a good night's sleep?" or "You're glowing! What's your secret?"
Imagine feeling like yourself again when you look in photos, instead of cringing and wondering when you started looking so... old.
That transformation is possible. And it has nothing to do with the expensive creams you've been using. 
In this presentation, I’m going to share the heartbreaking story of how I, a busy mom of two right here in Florida, discovered the real reason why every single eye cream had failed me… and why they're probably failing you, too.
And how a chance meeting with a leading anti-aging physician revealed the shocking scientific truth that the cosmetic industry doesn't want you to know.
You'll discover what's really happening at the cellular level that causes your eyes to age faster than the rest of your face. And why everything you've been told about collagen loss is missing the most critical piece of the puzzle.
I'm going to reveal why 97% of eye creams fail - and it's not what you think. You'll learn about the hidden breakdown happening at a microscopic level that no other product addresses, and why spending more money on "premium" eye creams often makes the problem worse, not better.
What I learned from this anti-aging physician with over 30 years of experience changed everything. His revelation was so profound, so different from anything I'd ever heard, that I knew I had to share it with every woman who's been through the same frustration I experienced.
This is specifically for women over 35 who are tired of wasting money and are ready for a real, science-backed solution that delivers visible results
Now, I know this might sound too good to be true, especially if you've been disappointed before. Trust me, I was the biggest skeptic of all after spending thousands of dollars and getting nowhere.
But when women like Carol, a 51-year-old from Texas, tells me that this breakthrough is "the holy grail of eye care" and that she looks 10 years younger...
When Elizabeth, 62, says her aesthetician was amazed at how youthful her eye area looks after just 4 months...
When Patricia, 54, tells me her eyes "couldn't be happier" and she actually looks forward to using this breakthrough every night...
I knew this wasn't just another false hope. This was a revolutionary shift in how to approach eye aging.
So if you're ready to finally understand why nothing has worked for you before, and discover the one approach that actually targets the root cause of eye aging, then please watch every word of this presentation.
Background Story
My name is Laura, and just like you, I'm a busy mom trying to juggle everything life throws at me. I live in Florida with my husband and our two kids, and for most of my thirties, I thought I was aging pretty gracefully.
Sure, I had the usual stresses - kids' schedules, work deadlines, trying to keep everyone fed and happy. But I felt good. I felt young. I felt like... me.
But then, around my 37th birthday, something shifted. It felt like it happened overnight.
I remember the moment so clearly. I was getting ready to go out for dinner with my husband, and I caught my reflection in the bathroom mirror under that bright, unforgiving light. And I just... stared. The face looking back at me looked exhausted. There were fine lines fanning out from my eyes that weren't just 'smile lines' anymore. They were deep-set crow's feet. And under my eyes, the skin looked thin, almost translucent, with purplish dark circles that made me look permanently worn out.
But it wasn't just the lines. The skin under my eyes looked... different. Loose. Crepey. Like it had lost some essential quality that made it look alive and youthful.
I stared at myself in that mirror and felt like I was looking at a stranger. This wasn't the face I knew. This wasn't how I felt inside.
That's when the obsession began.
I started with what everyone tries first - the drugstore creams. CeraVe, Olay, Neutrogena. I slathered them on religiously, morning and night, convinced that consistency was the key.
Nothing.
So I upgraded to the department store counter. Estée Lauder's "miraculous" eye cream for $85. Clinique's "proven" formula for $65. I even splurged on a tiny jar of La Mer eye cream that cost me $190 and lasted barely a month.
Still nothing.
The saleswomen were so convincing. They had charts and studies and before-and-after photos. They promised me that their latest breakthrough would be different, that this time I'd see real results.
But month after month, jar after jar, my reflection stayed the same. If anything, I was starting to look worse.
That's when I got desperate and made an appointment with a dermatologist. Surely a medical professional would have answers, right?
She recommended prescription retinoids that burned my delicate eye area. Then suggested laser treatments that cost $800 per session and required a week of downtime.
I tried them. The burning, the swelling, the expense... and for what? Minimal improvement that disappeared within months.
I even considered Botox, but the thought of injecting toxins around my eyes terrified me. Plus, at $500 every three to four months, it would cost me over $1,500 a year just to maintain results that wouldn't even address the skin texture and dark circles that bothered me most.
By this point, I'd easily spent over $3,000 trying to fix my eye area. Three thousand dollars! That could have been a family vacation, or money toward my kids' college funds. Instead, it was money down the drain with nothing to show for it.
But the financial cost wasn't even the worst part.
The worst part was watching myself disappear.
I stopped taking photos with my kids because I hated how I looked. I started avoiding mirrors whenever possible. I began wearing sunglasses indoors just to hide my eyes.
My husband would try to reassure me, saying I was being too hard on myself. But I could see it in his eyes too - a flicker of surprise when he looked at me, like he was also noticing the changes.
I felt like I was becoming invisible. Like the confident, vibrant woman I'd always been was fading away, replaced by someone who looked tired and old and... defeated.
That's when I realized something had to change. I couldn't keep living like this, couldn't keep throwing money at products that didn't work, couldn't keep watching myself age rapidly while feeling helpless to stop it.
I needed real answers. I needed to understand what was actually happening to my skin, not just get sold another "miracle" cream by someone who'd never experienced what I was going through.
So I started asking around. I talked to friends, searched online forums, reached out to anyone who might have insights beyond the standard beauty counter advice.
And that's when my friend Sarah mentioned Dr. Blaine Schilling.
"Laura," she said, "if anyone can give you real answers, it's Dr. Schilling. He's been treating aging for over 30 years, and he actually understands the science behind what's happening to your skin."
At that point, I was willing to try anything. So I made the call.
The Meeting with Dr. Schilling & UMP Reveal
Honestly, I walked into his office expecting another disappointing consultation. I was ready for him to recommend the same old things I'd already tried. But I was wrong.
He listened. Really listened as I told him about my journey, my frustrations, all the money I'd wasted on products that promised everything and delivered nothing.
And then he said something that stopped me in my tracks:
"Laura, everything you've tried has failed because every single product - from the cheapest drugstore cream to the most expensive department store miracle - is targeting the wrong problem. The entire beauty industry is focused on collagen loss. But that's only a tiny part of the story. The real issue, the one that causes the rapid aging around the eyes, is something I call Collagen Architecture Breakdown.
He gave me this incredible analogy that made it all make sense. He said, 'Think of young, healthy skin like a piece of high-quality fabric with a perfectly tight, organized weave. Every single collagen 'thread' is in its proper place, working together to create a smooth, strong, and firm surface.'"
But as we age, especially in the delicate skin around the eyes, something far more devastating happens than just losing a few threads. The entire structure starts to collapse. The threads 
He explained that this breakdown starts at a critical place called the Dermal-Epidermal Junction, or the DEJ. It's the place where your top layer of skin meets the deeper layer. When the architecture there collapses, it creates a chain reaction.
* The skin's support network can no longer hold its shape, causing it to fold and sag, creating wrinkles.
* The weakened structure allows blood vessels to show through the thinning skin, which is what we see as dark circles.
* And fluid begins to accumulate in the gaps where that organized structure used to provide proper drainage, leading to puffiness and under-eye bags."
It was a total 'aha!' moment. For the first time, I understood why my eyes were aging so fast. It wasn't just about needing more collagen. It was that the very foundation of my skin had become a disorganized mess. Pouring more collagen on top of that mess would be like throwing new threads onto a tangled pile of yarn and expecting it to become a sweater. It just doesn't work. I finally understood why every other cream had failed me…
Because if the problem is Collagen Architecture Breakdown, then the solution isn't to add more collagen to broken fabric. The solution is to restore the organized structure of the weave itself.

Dr. Schilling's Solution - UMS Reveal
And yet, even though I felt thrilled to finally understand why the skin around my eyes seemed to be aging so much faster than the rest of my face…
I was also worried, because what Dr. Schilling had described sounded like something that would be impossible to fix. But that's when Dr. Schilling's eyes lit up. He told me that after years of research, he had developed a theoretical framework for reversing this breakdown.
He called it 'The Structural Renewal System.' He said the breakthrough isn't to just add more collagen into that broken fabric. The secret is to command the skin to reorganize and rebuild the architecture it already has. To take those tangled, messy threads and weave them back into that tight, strong, youthful structure.
He broke it down for me into three simple, logical steps.
"Step One is what I call the Structural Renewal Signal. You need specific compounds that can penetrate deep to where the breakdown is occurring and essentially command your skin's machinery to reorganize the collagen architecture."
"These compounds act like a master weaver, telling the loose, tangled collagen fibers to pull tight and arrange themselves back into their proper structure."
"Step Two is the Targeted Repair Complex. While the renewal signal is reorganizing existing structure, you also need precise building blocks - specific amino acids that provide exactly what your skin needs to rebuild and strengthen that organized matrix."
"Not just any proteins or amino acids," he emphasized, "but the exact materials your skin uses to create strong, properly structured collagen."
"And Step Three is the Integrity Locking System. Once you've restored the proper architecture, you need to protect it from the enzymes that caused the breakdown in the first place."
"These are called matrix metalloproteinases - MMPs for short - and they're essentially little scissors that cut up your collagen structure. If you don't control them, all your renewal work gets undone.
It was the most brilliant, logical approach to skincare I had ever heard. It was based on real biology. Signal. Repair. Lock. It made perfect sense. I was so excited, I asked him, 'Okay, so what product do I buy? Where can I get this?'"
And that's when he gave me the bad news. He smiled kindly and told me that while the science was clear, no company was actually using this comprehensive approach. He said the big brands were too invested in their old 'just add collagen' formulas. He had given me the map, the scientific framework for what would actually work... but he told me I'd have to find—or create—the solution myself."
That conversation changed my life. I walked out of Dr. Schilling's office with knowledge that no one had ever shared with me before, but also with the daunting realization that if I wanted to solve my problem, I was going to have to do it myself.
But at least now I knew exactly what I was looking for.
Product Buildup + Reveal
Armed with Dr. Schilling's insights about Collagen Architecture Breakdown and the Structural Renewal System, I went on a mission.
I researched every eye cream on the market with new eyes, looking specifically for products that addressed the DEJ, that contained compounds capable of reorganizing collagen structure, that included MMP inhibitors to protect against future breakdown.
And guess what I found?
Nothing. Absolutely nothing.
Product after product claimed to boost collagen, but none addressed the architectural breakdown that was the real problem. They were all still stuck on surface-level solutions - adding moisture, providing temporary plumping, or using basic peptides that couldn't penetrate to where the real damage was occurring.
Even the most expensive, scientifically-formulated creams were missing the mark entirely.
I started reaching out to cosmetic chemists, asking if they could formulate something based on Dr. Schilling's specifications. Most of them had never even heard of the DEJ, let alone understood the importance of collagen architecture.
It was incredibly frustrating. Here I had the roadmap to the solution, but no one seemed capable of creating it.
That's when my husband suggested we try to develop it ourselves.
"Laura," he said, "you understand the science now better than most cosmetic companies do. You know exactly what needs to be done. Why don't we find the right people and create the product Dr. Schilling described?"
It seemed impossible at first. How could two regular people with no background in cosmetic formulation compete with massive companies that had been doing this for decades?
But then I realized something: those massive companies weren't trying to solve the real problem. They were making money selling temporary fixes and false hope. They had no incentive to create something that actually worked.
We, on the other hand, had every incentive in the world. I needed this solution to work, not just for me, but for my confidence, my self-esteem, my ability to feel like myself again.
So we started the process.
First, we had to find the right ingredients. Not just any collagen-boosting compounds, but specifically those that could signal structural renewal at the DEJ level.
We discovered Dipalmitoyl Hydroxyproline - a specialized peptide that had been shown in clinical studies to reduce wrinkles by 32% and increase skin firmness by 14%. But more importantly, it was one of the few compounds proven to stimulate the production of TIMPs - the proteins that inhibit those collagen-destroying MMPs Dr. Schilling had warned us about. This was our Step One - the Structural Renewal Signal.
Then we found the ingredients for Step Two - our Targeted Repair Complex. We discovered Pistacia Lentiscus extract, derived from mastic trees. Research showed it could increase the density of supporting fibers in the upper dermis by 51% while decreasing the weakened dermal layer by 29%.
But we also realized we needed the precise building blocks for collagen reconstruction. That's when we discovered the power of specific amino acids - Proline, Glycine, and Alanine. These aren't just any amino acids; they're the fundamental building blocks that comprise nearly 23% of collagen's structure. Clinical studies showed that when these amino acids are provided in the right concentrations, they serve as a catalyst for healthy collagen production, giving your skin the exact raw materials it needs to rebuild and repair the architectural damage at the DEJ level.
What made this discovery even more exciting was research showing that amino acid complexes could deliver an 8.955% decrease in wrinkle depth around the eyes - proving that providing these precise building blocks was essential for the structural renewal we were trying to achieve.
Finally, we needed Step Three - the Integrity Locking System to protect all this renewal work from future breakdown. That's where we incorporated powerful antioxidants like Vitamin C and E, which work synergistically to provide 4 to 8 times more protection against environmental damage. But the real breakthrough was realizing that the Dipalmitoyl Hydroxyproline didn't just signal renewal - it also continuously stimulated TIMP production, creating an ongoing protective shield against those collagen-destroying enzymes that had caused the original architectural breakdown.
But finding the right ingredients was only the beginning. We had to determine the exact concentrations, the optimal delivery system, the perfect pH levels to ensure these compounds could actually penetrate to the DEJ where they were needed.
There were so many setbacks. Our first formulations were too thick and couldn't absorb properly. Then we made them too thin and they didn't deliver enough active ingredients. We struggled with stability, with preservation, with creating something gentle enough for the delicate eye area but powerful enough to create real change.
Month after month, we tested and refined, tested and refined. I was starting to wonder if we'd bitten off more than we could chew.
And then, finally, we had our breakthrough.
The formulation team called me with excitement in their voices. "Laura, we think we've got it. This formula hits every marker Dr. Schilling specified. The penetration studies are incredible, the stability testing is perfect, and the initial user trials are showing results we've never seen before."
I was almost afraid to hope, but when I tried the final formula myself, I knew within the first week that something was different.
My eye area felt different - more supple, more hydrated, but in a way that seemed to come from deep within the skin rather than just on the surface.
By week three, I could see visible changes. The fine lines that had been etched around my eyes were softening. The dark circles were lightening. My skin was starting to regain that firmness I'd lost.
But the real test came at week six, when I ran into an old friend at the grocery store.
"Laura!" she exclaimed. "You look amazing! What have you been doing? You look so rested and... young!"
That's when I knew we had created something special.
I immediately sent photos and detailed notes to Dr. Schilling. His response was everything I'd hoped for:
"Laura, this is exactly what I was hoping someone would create. You've taken the theoretical framework of the Structural Renewal System and turned it into a practical, effective solution. I'm genuinely impressed with both the science and the results."
Word spread quickly among my friends and family. Everyone wanted to know my secret, wanted to try this "miracle" product I'd created.

Close - Product Details & Value Building

﻿Example #1: Peptide Eye Serum

TAM = Total Addressable U.S. Market 70MM People
1. Unaware (40%) A 38-year-old woman goes about her daily routine without noticing or thinking about the fine lines around her eyes. She might catch glimpses in mirrors but doesn't register any changes or concerns about aging. Eye cream isn't even on her radar - she uses basic moisturizer if anything.
Goal: From Point A (Prospect) To Point B (Buyer)

|___________|____________|__________|___________|__________|
Unaware -> Prob Aware -> Sol Aware -> Prod Aware ->Most Aware->Buy

2. Problem Aware (60%) She starts noticing crow's feet in photos or catches herself in harsh lighting and thinks "When did I start looking so tired?" She's aware something has changed around her eyes but doesn't know what to do about it. She might mention to friends that she's "starting to look older" but hasn't researched solutions.
3. Solution Aware (99%) She knows eye creams exist and that there are anti-aging treatments available. She's seen ads for various skincare products and knows people use things like retinol, hyaluronic acid, or get cosmetic procedures. She understands there are ways to address eye aging but doesn't know which approach is best or what specific products to consider.
4. Product Aware (13.5%) She's learned about peptides specifically for eye care and knows that peptide-based eye creams are a category of anti-aging products. She understands that peptides can help with collagen production and fine lines, and she's researching different peptide eye creams in general, but hasn't discovered your specific brand yet.
5. Most Aware (<1% - 1%) She knows about your specific peptide eye cream brand, has researched your company's approach, understands your unique formulation and benefits, has read reviews of your product specifically, and is ready to make a purchase decision about your brand versus competitors.

Example #2: Eco-Friendly Cleaning Products
1. Unaware A busy parent uses whatever cleaning products are cheapest at the grocery store without thinking about ingredients or environmental impact. They clean regularly but don't consider the connection between household cleaners and indoor air quality, skin irritation, or environmental harm.
2. Problem Aware They start noticing their child's skin reactions after cleaning day, or they read an article about indoor air pollution. They realize conventional cleaners might be causing issues in their home but don't know what alternatives exist.
3. Solution Aware They learn that "green" or "natural" cleaning products exist and that people are switching to safer alternatives. They see eco-friendly options in stores but feel overwhelmed by the choices and aren't sure what really works or what to look for.
4. Product Aware They understand that eco-friendly cleaning products are a legitimate category and know about plant-based formulas, non-toxic ingredients, and sustainable packaging. They're researching different eco-cleaning brands and comparing approaches.
5. Most Aware They know about your specific eco-friendly cleaning brand, understand your unique formulation philosophy, have read reviews of your products, and are deciding whether to switch from their current brand or try your starter kit.
Example #3: Personal Branding Mastermind
1. Unaware A mid-level professional focuses solely on doing good work, assuming that quality results will naturally lead to career advancement. They don't think about how they're perceived professionally or that reputation management is something they should actively work on.
2. Problem Aware They notice colleagues getting promoted over them, or they're not being considered for opportunities they feel qualified for. They realize that being good at their job isn't enough - something about visibility or perception is holding them back.
3. Solution Aware They learn that "personal branding" is a thing and that professionals actively work on their reputation, LinkedIn presence, and thought leadership. They understand this could help their career but don't know how to approach it strategically.
4. Product Aware They know that personal branding courses, masterminds, and coaching programs exist. They're familiar with the concept of building thought leadership, creating content, and networking strategically, and they're researching different educational options.
5. Most Aware They've found your specific personal branding mastermind, understand your methodology and community approach, have reviewed your curriculum and success stories, and are ready to invest in your program specifically.
Example #4: Meditation Program for Anxiety
1. Unaware Someone experiences stress, racing thoughts, or sleep issues but attributes it to being "busy" or having a "stressful job." They don't recognize these as anxiety symptoms or consider that there might be techniques to manage them.
2. Problem Aware They realize they're dealing with anxiety - maybe after a particularly difficult period or when someone points it out. They know they need help managing their mental state but don't know what approaches might work for them.
3. Solution Aware They've heard that meditation, mindfulness, therapy, or anxiety management techniques can help. They know these solutions exist but aren't sure which approach to try or how to get started effectively.
4. Product Aware They understand that meditation programs specifically designed for anxiety are available. They know about guided meditation apps, anxiety-focused courses, and structured mindfulness programs, and they're comparing different options.
5. Most Aware They've discovered your specific meditation program for anxiety, understand your approach and methodology, have read testimonials from people with similar anxiety challenges, and are ready to commit to your program.
Example #5: Tax Preparation for Freelancers
1. Unaware A new freelancer treats taxes the same way they did as an employee - maybe using basic tax software or going to a general tax preparer. They don't realize that freelancer taxes have unique complexities or opportunities for optimization.
2. Problem Aware They get hit with a big tax bill, miss out on deductions, or feel overwhelmed trying to organize their freelance income and expenses. They realize freelance taxes are more complicated than they thought but don't know what to do differently.
3. Solution Aware They learn that specialized tax help for freelancers exists - whether through specialized software, tax professionals who understand freelance work, or educational resources about freelance tax strategy.
4. Product Aware They know that freelance-specific tax preparation services are a category and understand the benefits of working with specialists who know about quarterly payments, business deductions, and freelance tax strategy.
5. Most Aware They've found your specific tax preparation service for freelancers, understand your expertise with their type of work, have reviewed your pricing and service offerings, and are ready to hire you for their tax needs.

﻿Prompt #1: 

I want your help evaluating the level of Market Awareness for a product in the YOUR NICHE space. The specific product is _PRODUCT_

I would like for you to dive deep to help me understand the current level of market awareness for this product in _GEOGRAPHY_. 

Optional:
Here are more details about the market _DETAILS_

To do this, we can look at the classic levels of Product and Market awareness that is often attributed to Eugene Schwarz, which can be categorized as follows:

1. Unaware: Prospects are not even aware of a problem or need that your product or service can solve.
2. Problem Aware: Prospects recognize they have a problem or need but are unaware of potential solutions.
3. Solution Aware: Prospects know that solutions exist for their problem, but they are not yet aware of your specific solution.
4. Product Aware: Prospects know about your solution, your product or service, and are evaluating its features and benefits.
5. Most Aware: Prospects are highly aware of your solution, its benefits, and are likely to make a purchase decision soon. 

For the intents of this exercise, let’s not consider Product Aware or Most Aware to be for our specific product and brand. Instead let’s consider it to be an awareness about similar/nearly identical products and brands that offer those products. 

In order to make this assessment please utilize a variety of signals including social media chatter, articles and blog posts, influencer content, search trends, any available sales data on the product category (and its growth), and so on. 

Additionally:

1. Please provide an overview of the estimated TAM (total addressable market) for this product. 

2. Please provide a rough estimate of what percentage of the TAM falls into each category of product/market awareness.

3. At the end of your review, please give me a FINAL selection for which stage of Product/Market Awareness the majority of individuals within the market fall. 

Thanks!

=================================

The specific product is _a coaching program and community that shows people how they can leasing a property long-term and then managing it as a short-term rental (with the property owner’s consent) _

I would like for you to dive deep to help me understand the current level of market awareness for this product in _The U.S_. 

To do this, we can look at the classic levels of Product and Market awareness that is often attributed to Eugene Schwarz, which can be categorized as follows:

1. Unaware: Prospects are not even aware of a problem or need that your product or service can solve.
2. Problem Aware: Prospects recognize they have a problem or need but are unaware of potential solutions.
3. Solution Aware: Prospects know that solutions exist for their problem, but they are not yet aware of your specific solution.
4. Product Aware: Prospects know about your solution, your product or service, and are evaluating its features and benefits.
5. Most Aware: Prospects are highly aware of your solution, its benefits, and are likely to make a purchase decision soon. 

For the intents of this exercise, let’s not consider Product Aware or Market Aware to be for our specific product and brand. Instead let’s consider it to be an awareness about similar/nearly identical products and brands that offer those products. 

In order to make this assessment please utilize a variety of signals including social media chatter, articles and blog posts, influencer content, search trends, any available sales data on the product category (and its growth), and so on. 

Additionally:

1. Please provide an overview of the estimated TAM (total addressable market) for this product. 

2. Please provide a rough estimate of what percentage of the TAM falls into each category of product/market awareness.

3. At the end of your review, please give me a FINAL selection for which stage of Product/Market Awareness the majority of individuals within the market fall. 

Thanks!

Example 2 Outputs:

https://docs.google.com/document/d/1dYxhy6oy7pWdcDFRQnQbRBNbtg3AaWJQV-2HRklhbx0/edit?usp=sharing

﻿RMBC II: MID-COURSE RECAP 

What We’ve Covered So Far

1. Overview of Copy + How It’s Applied in 2025
* The A to B Journey
* Platform Specific Copy
* Fundamentals of DR Copy

2. Deep Research
* Product/Market Awareness
* Competitor Research
* Psychographic Research
* Unified Research Document
* Ingredient Research (When Relevant)

3. Unique Mechanisms 
* Overview
* UM Ideation With LLMs
* UM Evaluation Process
* UM Expansion with Claude 
* Claude Project Setup for Unique Mechanisms

VSL Copy Part I: Understanding Structures, Elements, Etc.
* Breakdowns
* Long Form
* Medium Form
* Short Form
* Hooks
* ADHD Hook Video Ads
* In-Feed vs. On Page VSLs

Brief 2.0
* The old brief vs the New Brief
* The Brief 2.0 Generator (Claude Project)
* Brief Generation Examples

VSL Copy Part II 
* Setting Up Claude Project Recipes for Long, Medium, 3-7 Minute, and Short VSLs. 
* VSL Creation Walkthroughs and Examples:
Long, Medium, 3-7 Minutes, and Short

=====

Zooming Out Even More, Here Our The Steps of the Process:

Research
1. Product/Market Awareness Deep Research
2. Competitor Deep Research
3. Psychographic Research
4. Optional - Ingredient Research
-> Create Unified Research Document

Mechanism
1. UM Ideation
2. UM Shortlist
3. UM Evaluation/Ranking
4. UM Expansion
->Create Doc With Your UM in Expanded Copy Format

Brief 2.0 
1. Upload Unified Research Doc, UM Doc, Ingredient 2.Research (Optional) 
3. Create Brief in Claude Project
4. Provide Feedback and Modifications to Claude 
-> Create Expanded Brief 2.0

VSL Copy
1. Select VSL Copy Length (Long, Medium, 3-7 Minute, Short)
2. Upload Brief into Corresponding Claude Project
3. Request Outline
4. Review/Modify/Tweak
5. Create Copy
6. Edit Outputs
7. Create Additional Leads
-> Create Finished VSL(s) of Varying Lengths & With Multiple Leads and Hooks
